GAAP diluted EPS was $0.58 in the first quarter, up 32% compared to the prior year period. And on an adjusted basis, diluted EPS increased 58% to a record $0.63 compared to $0.40 in the first quarter of 2024. This was an excellent result. An excellent result considering the growth we have experienced.
